**Cursor**

–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–π –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å! –î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–∞–∑–±–µ—Ä—ë–º **React Spring** –ø–æ–¥—Ä–æ–±–Ω–æ! ÔøΩÔøΩ

## üöÄ **–ß—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–µ React Spring?**

**React Spring** ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ —Å–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∞ –¥–ª—è —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã—Ö –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–π –≤ React –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è—Ö. –û–Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–∞—Ö —Ñ–∏–∑–∏–∫–∏ –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω (spring physics), —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –µ—Å—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∏ –ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–Ω—ã–º–∏.

### **–ö–ª—é—á–µ–≤—ã–µ –æ—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏:**
- ‚úÖ **–§–∏–∑–∏–∫–∞ –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω** ‚Äî –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∏–º–∏—Ç–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç —Ä–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ–∏–∑–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å—ã
- ‚úÖ **–ü—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç `requestAnimationFrame` –∏ –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥
- ‚úÖ **–ì–∏–±–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ª—é–±—ã–µ CSS —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞
- ‚úÖ **TypeScript** ‚Äî –ø–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞ —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏
- ‚úÖ **–•—É–∫–∏** ‚Äî —É–¥–æ–±–Ω—ã–µ React —Ö—É–∫–∏ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–π

## üé® **–ü–æ—á–µ–º—É React Spring –ª—É—á—à–µ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç–æ–≤?**

### **–°—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å –∞–ª—å—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∞–º–∏:**

| –ë–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∞ | –ü–ª—é—Å—ã | –ú–∏–Ω—É—Å—ã |
|------------|-------|--------|
| **React Spring** | üèÜ –§–∏–∑–∏–∫–∞ –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω, –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –≥–∏–±–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å | –¢—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç –∏–∑—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è API |
| **Framer Motion** | –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π API, –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ã—Ö –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ | –ë–æ–ª—å—à–∏–π —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä –±–∞–Ω–¥–ª–∞ |
| **CSS Transitions** | –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ç–∞, –Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å | –û–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –≥–∏–±–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å |
| **Vanilla JS** | –ü–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª—å | –ú–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–¥–∞, —Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å |

## üîß **–£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∞ –∏ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞—è –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞:**

```bash
npm install @react-spring/web
# –∏–ª–∏
yarn add @react-spring/web
```

## üìö **–û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–ø—Ü–∏–∏ React Spring:**

### **1. useSpring ‚Äî –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è**
```typescript
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';

const AnimatedComponent = () => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: { opacity: 0, transform: 'translateY(20px)' },
    to: { opacity: 1, transform: 'translateY(0px)' },
    config: { tension: 300, friction: 20 }
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      –ê–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç
    </animated.div>
  );
};
```

### **2. useTrail ‚Äî –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏**
```typescript
const AnimatedList = ({ items }) => {
  const springs = useTrail(items.length, {
    from: { opacity: 0, x: -20 },
    to: { opacity: 1, x: 0 },
    delay: 100,
  });

  return (
    <div>
      {springs.map((spring, index) => (
        <animated.div key={index} style={spring}>
          {items[index]}
        </animated.div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};
```

### **3. useTransition ‚Äî –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è/–∏—Å—á–µ–∑–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏—è**
```typescript
const AnimatedItems = ({ items }) => {
  const transitions = useTransition(items, {
    from: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 },
    enter: { opacity: 1, scale: 1 },
    leave: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 },
  });

  return (
    <div>
      {transitions((style, item) => (
        <animated.div style={style}>
          {item}
        </animated.div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};
```

## üéØ **–î–ª—è –Ω–∞—à–µ–π –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞:**

```typescript
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';

const FlyingProduct = ({ 
  isVisible, 
  productImage, 
  startPosition, 
  endPosition, 
  onComplete 
}) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: {
      x: startPosition.x,
      y: startPosition.y,
      scale: 1,
      opacity: 1,
      rotate: 0,
    },
    to: {
      x: endPosition.x,
      y: endPosition.y,
      scale: 0.3,
      opacity: 0,
      rotate: 360,
    },
    config: {
      tension: 300,    // –ñ—ë—Å—Ç–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω—ã
      friction: 20,    // –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      mass: 1,         // –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞ (–≤–ª–∏—è–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω–µ—Ä—Ü–∏—é)
    },
    onRest: onComplete, // –ö–æ–ª–±—ç–∫ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏—è
  });

  if (!isVisible) return null;

  return (
    <animated.img
      src={productImage}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        zIndex: 9999,
        width: 60,
        height: 60,
        objectFit: 'cover',
        borderRadius: 8,
        pointerEvents: 'none',
        boxShadow: '0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
        ...spring, // –í—Å–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞
      }}
    />
  );
};
```

## üöÄ **–í–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–π:**

### **1. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã**
```typescript
// –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã –ø—Ä–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞
const CartIcon = ({ itemCount }) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    scale: itemCount > 0 ? 1.2 : 1,
    rotate: itemCount > 0 ? 360 : 0,
    config: { tension: 400, friction: 10 }
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      <ShoppingCart />
    </animated.div>
  );
};
```

### **2. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤**
```typescript
// –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
const ProductCard = ({ product, index }) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: { opacity: 0, y: 50 },
    to: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },
    delay: index * 100,
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      {/* –ö–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ */}
    </animated.div>
  );
};
```

### **3. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –º–æ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω**
```typescript
// –ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –º–æ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω
const Modal = ({ isOpen, children }) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    opacity: isOpen ? 1 : 0,
    scale: isOpen ? 1 : 0.8,
    config: { tension: 300, friction: 30 }
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      {children}
    </animated.div>
  );
};
```

### **4. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–æ–∫**
```typescript
// –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ —Å hover —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç–∞–º–∏
const AnimatedButton = ({ children, onClick }) => {
  const [spring, api] = useSpring(() => ({
    scale: 1,
    config: { tension: 400, friction: 10 }
  }));

  return (
    <animated.button
      style={spring}
      onMouseEnter={() => api.start({ scale: 1.05 })}
      onMouseLeave={() => api.start({ scale: 1 })}
      onClick={onClick}
    >
      {children}
    </animated.button>
  );
};
```

## ÔøΩÔøΩ **–ü—Ä–µ–∏–º—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –¥–ª—è –±—É–¥—É—â–µ–≥–æ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏—è:**

1. **–ö–æ–Ω—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –≤—Å–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –±—É–¥—É—Ç –≤ –µ–¥–∏–Ω–æ–º —Å—Ç–∏–ª–µ
2. **–ü—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥
3. **–ì–∏–±–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –ª–µ–≥–∫–æ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
4. **–¢–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è** ‚Äî –ø–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞ TypeScript
5. **–°–æ–æ–±—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ** ‚Äî –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞ –∏ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è

## üí° **–†–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥–∞—Ü–∏—è:**

**React Spring** ‚Äî –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–π –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä –¥–ª—è –¥–æ–ª–≥–æ—Å—Ä–æ—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–π –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–µ! –û–Ω –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª–∏—Ç —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å:
- üé® –ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥—ã –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–∞–º–∏
- ÔøΩÔøΩ –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã –∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
- üì± –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–∞
- üéØ –ú–∏–∫—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–ª—è —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–∏—è UX

–•–æ—á–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —è —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–ª –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é React Spring? üöÄ

```shellscript
npm install @react-spring/web
# –∏–ª–∏
yarn add @react-spring/web
```

import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';

const FlyingProduct = ({ 
  isVisible, 
  productImage, 
  startPosition, 
  endPosition, 
  onComplete 
}) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: {
      x: startPosition.x,
      y: startPosition.y,
      scale: 1,
      opacity: 1,
      rotate: 0,
    },
    to: {
      x: endPosition.x,
      y: endPosition.y,
      scale: 0.3,
      opacity: 0,
      rotate: 360,
    },
    config: {
      tension: 300,    // –ñ—ë—Å—Ç–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω—ã
      friction: 20,    // –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      mass: 1,         // –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞ (–≤–ª–∏—è–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω–µ—Ä—Ü–∏—é)
    },
    onRest: onComplete, // –ö–æ–ª–±—ç–∫ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏—è
  });

  if (!isVisible) return null;

  return (
    <animated.img
      src={productImage}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        zIndex: 9999,
        width: 60,
        height: 60,
        objectFit: 'cover',
        borderRadius: 8,
        pointerEvents: 'none',
        boxShadow: '0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
        ...spring, // –í—Å–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞
      }}
    />
  );
};
```

**Cursor**

–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ! –î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑—É–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é React Spring! ÔøΩÔøΩ

–°–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏–º –±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫—É:


–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ! –¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞:


```typescriptreact
import React from 'react';
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';

interface FlyingProductProps {
  isVisible: boolean;
  productImage: string;
  startPosition: { x: number; y: number };
  endPosition: { x: number; y: number };
  onComplete: () => void;
}

const FlyingProduct: React.FC<FlyingProductProps> = ({
  isVisible,
  productImage,
  startPosition,
  endPosition,
  onComplete,
}) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: {
      x: startPosition.x,
      y: startPosition.y,
      scale: 1,
      opacity: 1,
      rotate: 0,
    },
    to: {
      x: endPosition.x,
      y: endPosition.y,
      scale: 0.3,
      opacity: 0,
      rotate: 360,
    },
    config: {
      tension: 300,    // –ñ—ë—Å—Ç–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω—ã
      friction: 20,    // –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      mass: 1,         // –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞ (–≤–ª–∏—è–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ –∏–Ω–µ—Ä—Ü–∏—é)
    },
    onRest: onComplete, // –ö–æ–ª–±—ç–∫ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏—è
    immediate: !isVisible, // –ü—Ä–æ–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º
  });

  if (!isVisible) return null;

  return (
    <animated.img
      src={productImage}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        zIndex: 9999,
        width: 60,
        height: 60,
        objectFit: 'cover',
        borderRadius: 8,
        pointerEvents: 'none',
        boxShadow: '0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
        ...spring, // –í—Å–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞
      }}
      alt="Flying product"
    />
  );
};

export default FlyingProduct;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º —Ö—É–∫ –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π:


```typescript
import { useState, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';

interface Position {
  x: number;
  y: number;
}

interface UseFlyingAnimationReturn {
  isFlying: boolean;
  flyingPosition: {
    start: Position | null;
    end: Position | null;
  };
  productImage: string | null;
  triggerAnimation: (productImage: string, startElement: HTMLElement, endElement: HTMLElement) => void;
  resetAnimation: () => void;
}

export const useFlyingAnimation = (): UseFlyingAnimationReturn => {
  const [isFlying, setIsFlying] = useState(false);
  const [flyingPosition, setFlyingPosition] = useState<{
    start: Position | null;
    end: Position | null;
  }>({ start: null, end: null });
  const [productImage, setProductImage] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const triggerAnimation = useCallback((
    image: string,
    startElement: HTMLElement,
    endElement: HTMLElement
  ) => {
    // –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–∏ —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤
    const startRect = startElement.getBoundingClientRect();
    const endRect = endElement.getBoundingClientRect();

    // –£—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
    setFlyingPosition({
      start: {
        x: startRect.left + startRect.width / 2 - 30, // –¶–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∏–∑–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ
        y: startRect.top + startRect.height / 2 - 30,
      },
      end: {
        x: endRect.left + endRect.width / 2 - 15, // –¶–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω–µ
        y: endRect.top + endRect.height / 2 - 15,
      },
    });

    setProductImage(image);
    setIsFlying(true);
  }, []);

  const resetAnimation = useCallback(() => {
    setIsFlying(false);
    setFlyingPosition({ start: null, end: null });
    setProductImage(null);
  }, []);

  return {
    isFlying,
    flyingPosition,
    productImage,
    triggerAnimation,
    resetAnimation,
  };
};
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏–º Header, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å ref –¥–ª—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useState, forwardRef } from 'react';
import {
  AppBar,
  Toolbar,
  Typography,
  IconButton,
  Badge,
  Box,
  Button,
  Menu,
  MenuItem,
} from '@mui/material';
import {
  ShoppingCart,
  AccountCircle,
  Agriculture,
  Language,
  AdminPanelSettings,
} from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppSelector, useAppDispatch } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { toggleCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { clearUser } from '../../store/slices/userSlice';
import { setLanguage, type Language as LanguageType } from '../../store/slices/languageSlice';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

interface HeaderProps {
  onProfileClick?: () => void;
  showOnWelcome?: boolean;
  cartRef?: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement>;
}

const Header: React.FC<HeaderProps> = ({ 
  onProfileClick, 
  showOnWelcome = true,
  cartRef 
}) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const cartItems = useAppSelector(state => state.cart.items);
  const user = useAppSelector(state => state.user.user);
  const currentLanguage = useAppSelector(state => state.language.currentLanguage);
  const [langAnchor, setLangAnchor] = React.useState<null | HTMLElement>(null);
  const [profileAnchor, setProfileAnchor] = useState<null | HTMLElement>(null);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const savedLanguage = localStorage.getItem('language') as LanguageType;
    if (savedLanguage) {
      dispatch(setLanguage(savedLanguage));
    }
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —è–∑—ã–∫–∞ —Å i18n
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (currentLanguage && i18n.language !== currentLanguage && i18n.isInitialized) {
      i18n.changeLanguage(currentLanguage);
    }
  }, [currentLanguage]);

  const handleCartClick = () => {
    dispatch(toggleCart());
  };

  const handleLanguageClick = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLElement>) => {
    setLangAnchor(event.currentTarget);
  };

  const handleLanguageClose = () => {
    setLangAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleLanguageSelect = (language: LanguageType) => {
    dispatch(setLanguage(language));
    localStorage.setItem('language', language);
    if (i18n.isInitialized) {
      i18n.changeLanguage(language);
    }
    setLangAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleProfileMenu = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLElement>) => {
    if (user) {
      setProfileAnchor(event.currentTarget);
    } else if (onProfileClick) {
      onProfileClick();
    }
  };

  const handleProfileClose = () => {
    setProfileAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    dispatch(clearUser());
    setProfileAnchor(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('jwt');
  };

  return (
    <AppBar position="static" sx={{ backgroundColor: '#4CAF50' }}>
      <Toolbar>
        {/* üåæ –õ–æ–≥–æ */}
        <Agriculture sx={{ mr: 2 }} />
        <Typography variant="h6" component="div" sx={{ flexGrow: 1 }}>
          ◊©◊ï◊ß ◊î◊ó◊ß◊ú◊ê◊ô üáÆüá± Farmer Market
        </Typography>

        {/* üåê –Ø–∑—ã–∫–∏ */}
        <IconButton color="inherit" onClick={handleLanguageClick}>
          <Language />
        </IconButton>
        <Menu
          anchorEl={langAnchor}
          open={Boolean(langAnchor)}
          onClose={handleLanguageClose}
        >
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('he')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'he'}
          >
            üáÆüá± ◊¢◊ë◊®◊ô◊™
          </MenuItem>
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('en')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'en'}
          >
            üá∫üá∏ English
          </MenuItem>
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('ru')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'ru'}
          >
            üá∑üá∫ –†—É—Å—Å–∫–∏–π
          </MenuItem>
        </Menu>

        {/* üõí –ö–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω–∞ */}
        <IconButton 
          ref={cartRef}
          color="inherit" 
          onClick={handleCartClick}
        >
          <Badge badgeContent={cartItems.length} color="error">
            <ShoppingCart />
          </Badge>
        </IconButton>

        {/* üõ†Ô∏è –ê–¥–º–∏–Ω–∫–∞ */}
        <IconButton 
          color="inherit" 
          onClick={() => window.open('/admin', '_blank')}
          title="–ü–∞–Ω–µ–ª—å –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞"
        >
          <AdminPanelSettings />
        </IconButton>

        {/* üë§ –ü—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª—å */}
        <IconButton color="inherit" onClick={handleProfileMenu}>
          <AccountCircle />
        </IconButton>
        <Menu
          anchorEl={profileAnchor}
          open={Boolean(profileAnchor)}
          onClose={handleProfileClose}
        >
          {user && (
            <>
              <MenuItem disabled>
                {user.name ? user.name : user.email}
              </MenuItem>
              <MenuItem onClick={() => { handleProfileClose(); navigate('/orders'); }}>–ò—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤</MenuItem>
              <MenuItem onClick={handleLogout}>{t('logout')}</MenuItem>
            </>
          )}
        </Menu>
      </Toolbar>
    </AppBar>
  );
};

export default Header;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏–º ProductCatalog, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import Grid from '@mui/material/Grid';
import {
  Card,
  CardMedia,
  CardContent,
  Typography,
  Button,
  Chip,
  Box,
  TextField,
  InputAdornment,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
} from '@mui/material';

import { Search, Add, Spa, Store } from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { fetchProducts, setSearchTerm, setSelectedCategory } from '../../store/slices/productsSlice';
import { addToCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { Product, ProductCategory } from '../../types';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useFlyingAnimation } from '../../hooks/useFlyingAnimation';
import FlyingProduct from '../common/FlyingProduct';

const ProductCatalog: React.FC = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const { items, loading, selectedCategory, searchTerm } = useAppSelector(state => state.products);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  
  // –•—É–∫ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞
  const {
    isFlying,
    flyingPosition,
    productImage,
    triggerAnimation,
    resetAnimation,
  } = useFlyingAnimation();

  // Ref –¥–ª—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã –≤ Header
  const cartRef = useRef<HTMLButtonElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchProducts());
  }, [dispatch]);

  const filteredProducts = items.filter(product => {
    const p = product as any;
    const matchesCategory = !selectedCategory || p.category === selectedCategory;
    const search = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
    const matchesSearch =
      (typeof p.nameRu === 'string' && p.nameRu.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
      (typeof p.nameEn === 'string' && p.nameEn.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
      (typeof p.nameHe === 'string' && p.nameHe.includes(search));
    return matchesCategory && matchesSearch;
  });

  const handleAddToCart = (product: Product, cardElement: HTMLElement) => {
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é
    if (cartRef.current) {
      triggerAnimation(product.image, cardElement, cartRef.current);
    }
    
    // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
    dispatch(addToCart(product));
  };

  const getCategoryEmoji = (category: ProductCategory) => {
    const emojis = {
      [ProductCategory.VEGETABLES]: 'ü•¨',
      [ProductCategory.FRUITS]: 'üçé',
      [ProductCategory.HERBS]: 'üåø',
      [ProductCategory.DAIRY]: 'ü•õ',
      [ProductCategory.HONEY]: 'üçØ',
      [ProductCategory.FLOWERS]: 'üå∏',
    };
    return emojis[category] || 'üåæ';
  };

  const lang = i18n.language || 'en';

  return (
    <Box sx={{ padding: 3 }}>
      {/* üîç –§–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä—ã */}
      <Box sx={{ mb: 3, display: 'flex', gap: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <TextField
          placeholder={t('search_products')}
          value={searchTerm}
          onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSearchTerm(e.target.value))}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <Search />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
          sx={{
            minWidth: 300,
            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)',
            boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)',
            borderRadius: 2,
            '& .MuiInputBase-root': {
              borderRadius: 2,
              background: 'transparent',
            },
          }}
        />
        
        <FormControl sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}>
          <InputLabel>{t('category')}</InputLabel>
          <Select
            value={selectedCategory || ''}
            onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSelectedCategory(e.target.value || null))}
            label={t('category')}
          >
            <MenuItem value="">{t('all_categories')}</MenuItem>
            {Object.values(ProductCategory).map((category) => (
              <MenuItem key={category} value={category}>
                {getCategoryEmoji(category)} {category}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Box>

      {/* üì¶ –ö–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ–≥ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ */}
      <Grid container spacing={3} justifyContent="center">
        {filteredProducts.map((product) => {
          const p = product as any; // –¥–ª—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –∫ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º –ø–æ–ª—è–º
          const lang = i18n.language || 'en';
          const name =
            (typeof p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.nameEn || p.nameRu || p.nameHe || '';
          const description =
            (typeof p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.descriptionEn || p.descriptionRu || p.descriptionHe || '';
          
          return (
            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={p.id}>
              <Card 
                sx={{ 
                  height: '100%', 
                  display: 'flex', 
                  flexDirection: 'column',
                  transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.2s ease-in-out',
                  '&:hover': {
                    transform: 'translateY(-4px)',
                    boxShadow: '0 8px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
                  }
                }}
              >
                <CardMedia
                  component="img"
                  height="200"
                  image={p.image}
                  alt={name}
                />
                <CardContent sx={{ flexGrow: 1 }}>
                  <Typography variant="h6" component="h2" gutterBottom>
                    {getCategoryEmoji(p.category)} {name}
                  </Typography>
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" gutterBottom>
                    {description}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1, mb: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                    {p.organic && (
                      <Chip icon={<Spa />} label="Organic" size="small" color="success" />
                    )}
                    <Chip icon={<Store />} label={p.farmName} size="small" variant="outlined" />
                  </Box>
                  
                  <Typography variant="h6" color="primary" gutterBottom>
                    ‚Ç™{p.price} / {p.unit}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary">
                    üìç {p.location}
                  </Typography>
                </CardContent>
                
                <Box sx={{ p: 2, pt: 0 }}>
                  <Button
                    fullWidth
                    variant="contained"
                    startIcon={<Add />}
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      const cardElement = e.currentTarget.closest('.MuiCard-root') as HTMLElement;
                      if (cardElement) {
                        handleAddToCart(product, cardElement);
                      }
                    }}
                    disabled={!product.inStock}
                    sx={{ 
                      backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
                      transition: 'all 0.2s ease-in-out',
                      '&:hover': {
                        backgroundColor: '#45a049',
                        transform: 'scale(1.02)',
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    {product.inStock ? t('add_to_cart') : '◊ê◊ñ◊ú ◊ë◊û◊ú◊ê◊ô Out of Stock'}
                  </Button>
                </Box>
              </Card>
            </Grid>
          );
        })}
      </Grid>

      {/* üéØ –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ */}
      {isFlying && flyingPosition.start && flyingPosition.end && productImage && (
        <FlyingProduct
          isVisible={isFlying}
          productImage={productImage}
          startPosition={flyingPosition.start}
          endPosition={flyingPosition.end}
          onComplete={resetAnimation}
        />
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default ProductCatalog;
```

–ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—é –æ—à–∏–±–∫—É —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏:


```typescriptreact
          <Select
            value={selectedCategory || ''}
            onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSelectedCategory(e.target.value || null))}
            label={t('category')}
          >

->

          <Select
            value={selectedCategory || ''}
            onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSelectedCategory(e.target.value as ProductCategory || null))}
            label={t('category')}
          >
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—å App.tsx, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç—å ref –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã –≤ Header:


```typescriptreact
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Provider } from 'react-redux';
import { ThemeProvider, createTheme } from '@mui/material/styles';
import { CssBaseline } from '@mui/material';
import { store } from './store';
import WelcomeScreen from './components/pages/WelcomeScreen';
import WelcomePage from './components/pages/WelcomePage';
import ProductCatalog from './components/pages/ProductCatalog';
import CheckoutPage from './components/pages/CheckoutPage';
import AdminPage from './components/pages/AdminPage';
import SellerStubPage from './components/pages/SellerStubPage';
import OrderHistory from './components/pages/OrderHistory';
import CartDrawer from './components/common/CartDrawer';
import Header from './components/layout/Header';
import { useAppSelector, useAppDispatch } from './hooks/redux';
import { setToken } from './store/slices/userSlice';
import backgroundImage from './assets/images/Farm Sharing background.jpg';

// –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë–º —Ç–µ–º—É —Å –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–æ–π –∏–≤—Ä–∏—Ç–∞
const theme = createTheme({
  palette: {
    primary: {
      main: '#4CAF50',
    },
    secondary: {
      main: '#FF9800',
    },
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: [
      'Roboto',
      'Arial',
      'sans-serif',
      'Arial Hebrew',
      'David',
    ].join(','),
  },
  direction: 'ltr', // –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞ 'rtl' –¥–ª—è –∏–≤—Ä–∏—Ç–∞
});

const AppContent: React.FC = () => {
  const user = useAppSelector(state => state.user.user);
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  // useNavigate –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥–æ–≤
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('jwt');
    if (token) {
      dispatch(setToken(token));
    }
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∏–Ω–≥ –¥–ª—è –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∫–∏
  if (window.location.pathname === '/admin') {
    return <AdminPage />;
  }

  return (
    <Routes>
      <Route path="/" element={<WelcomeScreen onBuyerClick={() => navigate('/welcome')} onSellerClick={() => navigate('/seller')} />} />
      <Route path="/welcome" element={<WelcomePage onLoginClick={() => navigate('/catalog')} onRegisterClick={() => navigate('/catalog')} onBack={() => navigate('/')} />} />
      <Route path="/catalog" element={
        <div
          className="App"
          style={{
            backgroundImage: `url(${backgroundImage})`,
            backgroundSize: 'cover',
            backgroundPosition: 'center',
            backgroundRepeat: 'no-repeat',
            backgroundAttachment: 'fixed',
            minHeight: '100vh'
          }}
        >
          <div className="content-wrapper">
            <ProductCatalog />
            <CartDrawer />
          </div>
        </div>
      } />
      <Route path="/seller" element={<SellerStubPage onBack={() => navigate('/')} />} />
      <Route path="/orders" element={<OrderHistory />} />
    </Routes>
  );
};

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <Provider store={store}>
      <ThemeProvider theme={theme}>
        <CssBaseline />
        <Router>
          <AppContent />
        </Router>
      </ThemeProvider>
    </Provider>
  );
};

export default App;
```

–ú–Ω–µ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç-–æ–±—ë—Ä—Ç–∫—É –¥–ª—è –∫–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ–≥–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å ref –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useRef } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import Header from '../layout/Header';
import ProductCatalog from './ProductCatalog';
import backgroundImage from '../../assets/images/Farm Sharing background.jpg';

const CatalogPage: React.FC = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const cartRef = useRef<HTMLButtonElement>(null);

  return (
    <div
      className="App"
      style={{
        backgroundImage: `url(${backgroundImage})`,
        backgroundSize: 'cover',
        backgroundPosition: 'center',
        backgroundRepeat: 'no-repeat',
        backgroundAttachment: 'fixed',
        minHeight: '100vh'
      }}
    >
      <div className="content-wrapper">
        <Header 
          onProfileClick={() => navigate('/welcome')} 
          showOnWelcome={false}
          cartRef={cartRef}
        />
        <ProductCatalog cartRef={cartRef} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CatalogPage;
```

–ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—é —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –∏ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—é ProductCatalog:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import Grid from '@mui/material/Grid';
import {
  Card,
  CardMedia,
  CardContent,
  Typography,
  Button,
  Chip,
  Box,
  TextField,
  InputAdornment,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
} from '@mui/material';

import { Search, Add, Spa, Store } from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { fetchProducts, setSearchTerm, setSelectedCategory } from '../../store/slices/productsSlice';
import { addToCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { Product, ProductCategory } from '../../types';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useFlyingAnimation } from '../../hooks/useFlyingAnimation';
import FlyingProduct from '../common/FlyingProduct';

interface ProductCatalogProps {
  cartRef: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement>;
}

const ProductCatalog: React.FC<ProductCatalogProps> = ({ cartRef }) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const { items, loading, selectedCategory, searchTerm } = useAppSelector(state => state.products);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  
  // –•—É–∫ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞
  const {
    isFlying,
    flyingPosition,
    productImage,
    triggerAnimation,
    resetAnimation,
  } = useFlyingAnimation();

  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchProducts());
  }, [dispatch]);

  const filteredProducts = items.filter(product => {
    const p = product as any;
    const matchesCategory = !selectedCategory || p.category === selectedCategory;
    const search = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
    const matchesSearch =
      (typeof p.nameRu === 'string' && p.nameRu.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
      (typeof p.nameEn === 'string' && p.nameEn.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
      (typeof p.nameHe === 'string' && p.nameHe.includes(search));
    return matchesCategory && matchesSearch;
  });

  const handleAddToCart = (product: Product, cardElement: HTMLElement) => {
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é
    if (cartRef.current) {
      triggerAnimation(product.image, cardElement, cartRef.current);
    }
    
    // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
    dispatch(addToCart(product));
  };

  const getCategoryEmoji = (category: ProductCategory) => {
    const emojis = {
      [ProductCategory.VEGETABLES]: 'ü•¨',
      [ProductCategory.FRUITS]: 'üçé',
      [ProductCategory.HERBS]: 'üåø',
      [ProductCategory.DAIRY]: 'ü•õ',
      [ProductCategory.HONEY]: 'üçØ',
      [ProductCategory.FLOWERS]: 'üå∏',
    };
    return emojis[category] || 'üåæ';
  };

  const lang = i18n.language || 'en';

  return (
    <Box sx={{ padding: 3 }}>
      {/* üîç –§–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä—ã */}
      <Box sx={{ mb: 3, display: 'flex', gap: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <TextField
          placeholder={t('search_products')}
          value={searchTerm}
          onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSearchTerm(e.target.value))}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <Search />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
          sx={{
            minWidth: 300,
            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)',
            boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)',
            borderRadius: 2,
            '& .MuiInputBase-root': {
              borderRadius: 2,
              background: 'transparent',
            },
          }}
        />
        
        <FormControl sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}>
          <InputLabel>{t('category')}</InputLabel>
          <Select
            value={selectedCategory || ''}
            onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSelectedCategory(e.target.value as ProductCategory || null))}
            label={t('category')}
          >
            <MenuItem value="">{t('all_categories')}</MenuItem>
            {Object.values(ProductCategory).map((category) => (
              <MenuItem key={category} value={category}>
                {getCategoryEmoji(category)} {category}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Box>

      {/* üì¶ –ö–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ–≥ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ */}
      <Grid container spacing={3} justifyContent="center">
        {filteredProducts.map((product) => {
          const p = product as any; // –¥–ª—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –∫ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º –ø–æ–ª—è–º
          const lang = i18n.language || 'en';
          const name =
            (typeof p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.nameEn || p.nameRu || p.nameHe || '';
          const description =
            (typeof p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.descriptionEn || p.descriptionRu || p.descriptionHe || '';
          
          return (
            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={p.id}>
              <Card 
                sx={{ 
                  height: '100%', 
                  display: 'flex', 
                  flexDirection: 'column',
                  transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.2s ease-in-out',
                  '&:hover': {
                    transform: 'translateY(-4px)',
                    boxShadow: '0 8px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
                  }
                }}
              >
                <CardMedia
                  component="img"
                  height="200"
                  image={p.image}
                  alt={name}
                />
                <CardContent sx={{ flexGrow: 1 }}>
                  <Typography variant="h6" component="h2" gutterBottom>
                    {getCategoryEmoji(p.category)} {name}
                  </Typography>
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" gutterBottom>
                    {description}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1, mb: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                    {p.organic && (
                      <Chip icon={<Spa />} label="Organic" size="small" color="success" />
                    )}
                    <Chip icon={<Store />} label={p.farmName} size="small" variant="outlined" />
                  </Box>
                  
                  <Typography variant="h6" color="primary" gutterBottom>
                    ‚Ç™{p.price} / {p.unit}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary">
                    üìç {p.location}
                  </Typography>
                </CardContent>
                
                <Box sx={{ p: 2, pt: 0 }}>
                  <Button
                    fullWidth
                    variant="contained"
                    startIcon={<Add />}
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      const cardElement = e.currentTarget.closest('.MuiCard-root') as HTMLElement;
                      if (cardElement) {
                        handleAddToCart(product, cardElement);
                      }
                    }}
                    disabled={!product.inStock}
                    sx={{ 
                      backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
                      transition: 'all 0.2s ease-in-out',
                      '&:hover': {
                        backgroundColor: '#45a049',
                        transform: 'scale(1.02)',
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    {product.inStock ? t('add_to_cart') : '◊ê◊ñ◊ú ◊ë◊û◊ú◊ê◊ô Out of Stock'}
                  </Button>
                </Box>
              </Card>
            </Grid>
          );
        })}
      </Grid>

      {/* üéØ –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ */}
      {isFlying && flyingPosition.start && flyingPosition.end && productImage && (
        <FlyingProduct
          isVisible={isFlying}
          productImage={productImage}
          startPosition={flyingPosition.start}
          endPosition={flyingPosition.end}
          onComplete={resetAnimation}
        />
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default ProductCatalog;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—é App.tsx, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–π CatalogPage:


```typescriptreact
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Provider } from 'react-redux';
import { ThemeProvider, createTheme } from '@mui/material/styles';
import { CssBaseline } from '@mui/material';
import { store } from './store';
import WelcomeScreen from './components/pages/WelcomeScreen';
import WelcomePage from './components/pages/WelcomePage';
import CatalogPage from './components/pages/CatalogPage';
import CheckoutPage from './components/pages/CheckoutPage';
import AdminPage from './components/pages/AdminPage';
import SellerStubPage from './components/pages/SellerStubPage';
import OrderHistory from './components/pages/OrderHistory';
import CartDrawer from './components/common/CartDrawer';
import { useAppSelector, useAppDispatch } from './hooks/redux';
import { setToken } from './store/slices/userSlice';

// –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë–º —Ç–µ–º—É —Å –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–æ–π –∏–≤—Ä–∏—Ç–∞
const theme = createTheme({
  palette: {
    primary: {
      main: '#4CAF50',
    },
    secondary: {
      main: '#FF9800',
    },
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: [
      'Roboto',
      'Arial',
      'sans-serif',
      'Arial Hebrew',
      'David',
    ].join(','),
  },
  direction: 'ltr', // –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞ 'rtl' –¥–ª—è –∏–≤—Ä–∏—Ç–∞
});

const AppContent: React.FC = () => {
  const user = useAppSelector(state => state.user.user);
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('jwt');
    if (token) {
      dispatch(setToken(token));
    }
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –ü—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–π —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∏–Ω–≥ –¥–ª—è –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∫–∏
  if (window.location.pathname === '/admin') {
    return <AdminPage />;
  }

  return (
    <Routes>
      <Route path="/" element={<WelcomeScreen onBuyerClick={() => navigate('/welcome')} onSellerClick={() => navigate('/seller')} />} />
      <Route path="/welcome" element={<WelcomePage onLoginClick={() => navigate('/catalog')} onRegisterClick={() => navigate('/catalog')} onBack={() => navigate('/')} />} />
      <Route path="/catalog" element={<CatalogPage />} />
      <Route path="/seller" element={<SellerStubPage onBack={() => navigate('/')} />} />
      <Route path="/orders" element={<OrderHistory />} />
    </Routes>
  );
};

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <Provider store={store}>
      <ThemeProvider theme={theme}>
        <CssBaseline />
        <Router>
          <AppContent />
        </Router>
      </ThemeProvider>
    </Provider>
  );
};

export default App;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å CartDrawer –≤ CatalogPage:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useRef } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import Header from '../layout/Header';
import ProductCatalog from './ProductCatalog';
import CartDrawer from '../common/CartDrawer';
import backgroundImage from '../../assets/images/Farm Sharing background.jpg';

const CatalogPage: React.FC = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const cartRef = useRef<HTMLButtonElement>(null);

  return (
    <div
      className="App"
      style={{
        backgroundImage: `url(${backgroundImage})`,
        backgroundSize: 'cover',
        backgroundPosition: 'center',
        backgroundRepeat: 'no-repeat',
        backgroundAttachment: 'fixed',
        minHeight: '100vh'
      }}
    >
      <div className="content-wrapper">
        <Header 
          onProfileClick={() => navigate('/welcome')} 
          showOnWelcome={false}
          cartRef={cartRef}
        />
        <ProductCatalog cartRef={cartRef} />
        <CartDrawer />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CatalogPage;
```

–ò—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—é —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –≤ Header –∏ ProductCatalog:


```typescriptreact
interface HeaderProps {
  onProfileClick?: () => void;
  showOnWelcome?: boolean;
  cartRef?: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>;
}
```

```typescriptreact
interface ProductCatalogProps {
  cartRef: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>;
}
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é! –ó–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏–º –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ:


–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ! –¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—É—é –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –¥–ª—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –æ–Ω–∞ "–æ–∂–∏–≤–∞–ª–∞" –ø—Ä–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞:


```typescriptreact
import React from 'react';
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';
import { Badge, IconButton } from '@mui/material';
import { ShoppingCart } from '@mui/icons-material';

interface AnimatedCartIconProps {
  itemCount: number;
  onClick: () => void;
  ref?: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement>;
}

const AnimatedCartIcon: React.FC<AnimatedCartIconProps> = ({ 
  itemCount, 
  onClick, 
  ref 
}) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    scale: itemCount > 0 ? 1.1 : 1,
    rotate: itemCount > 0 ? 360 : 0,
    config: { 
      tension: 400, 
      friction: 10,
      mass: 0.8
    }
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      <IconButton 
        ref={ref}
        color="inherit" 
        onClick={onClick}
        sx={{
          transition: 'all 0.2s ease-in-out',
          '&:hover': {
            transform: 'scale(1.05)',
          }
        }}
      >
        <Badge badgeContent={itemCount} color="error">
          <ShoppingCart />
        </Badge>
      </IconButton>
    </animated.div>
  );
};

export default AnimatedCartIcon;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–∏–º Header, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—É—é –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫—É –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useState, forwardRef } from 'react';
import {
  AppBar,
  Toolbar,
  Typography,
  IconButton,
  Badge,
  Box,
  Button,
  Menu,
  MenuItem,
} from '@mui/material';
import {
  AccountCircle,
  Agriculture,
  Language,
  AdminPanelSettings,
} from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppSelector, useAppDispatch } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { toggleCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { clearUser } from '../../store/slices/userSlice';
import { setLanguage, type Language as LanguageType } from '../../store/slices/languageSlice';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import AnimatedCartIcon from '../common/AnimatedCartIcon';

interface HeaderProps {
  onProfileClick?: () => void;
  showOnWelcome?: boolean;
  cartRef?: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>;
}

const Header: React.FC<HeaderProps> = ({ 
  onProfileClick, 
  showOnWelcome = true,
  cartRef 
}) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const cartItems = useAppSelector(state => state.cart.items);
  const user = useAppSelector(state => state.user.user);
  const currentLanguage = useAppSelector(state => state.language.currentLanguage);
  const [langAnchor, setLangAnchor] = React.useState<null | HTMLElement>(null);
  const [profileAnchor, setProfileAnchor] = useState<null | HTMLElement>(null);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const savedLanguage = localStorage.getItem('language') as LanguageType;
    if (savedLanguage) {
      dispatch(setLanguage(savedLanguage));
    }
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è —è–∑—ã–∫–∞ —Å i18n
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (currentLanguage && i18n.language !== currentLanguage && i18n.isInitialized) {
      i18n.changeLanguage(currentLanguage);
    }
  }, [currentLanguage]);

  const handleCartClick = () => {
    dispatch(toggleCart());
  };

  const handleLanguageClick = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLElement>) => {
    setLangAnchor(event.currentTarget);
  };

  const handleLanguageClose = () => {
    setLangAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleLanguageSelect = (language: LanguageType) => {
    dispatch(setLanguage(language));
    localStorage.setItem('language', language);
    if (i18n.isInitialized) {
      i18n.changeLanguage(language);
    }
    setLangAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleProfileMenu = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLElement>) => {
    if (user) {
      setProfileAnchor(event.currentTarget);
    } else if (onProfileClick) {
      onProfileClick();
    }
  };

  const handleProfileClose = () => {
    setProfileAnchor(null);
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    dispatch(clearUser());
    setProfileAnchor(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('jwt');
  };

  return (
    <AppBar position="static" sx={{ backgroundColor: '#4CAF50' }}>
      <Toolbar>
        {/* üåæ –õ–æ–≥–æ */}
        <Agriculture sx={{ mr: 2 }} />
        <Typography variant="h6" component="div" sx={{ flexGrow: 1 }}>
          ◊©◊ï◊ß ◊î◊ó◊ß◊ú◊ê◊ô üáÆüá± Farmer Market
        </Typography>

        {/* üåê –Ø–∑—ã–∫–∏ */}
        <IconButton color="inherit" onClick={handleLanguageClick}>
          <Language />
        </IconButton>
        <Menu
          anchorEl={langAnchor}
          open={Boolean(langAnchor)}
          onClose={handleLanguageClose}
        >
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('he')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'he'}
          >
            üáÆüá± ◊¢◊ë◊®◊ô◊™
          </MenuItem>
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('en')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'en'}
          >
            üá∫üá∏ English
          </MenuItem>
          <MenuItem 
            onClick={() => handleLanguageSelect('ru')}
            selected={currentLanguage === 'ru'}
          >
            üá∑üá∫ –†—É—Å—Å–∫–∏–π
          </MenuItem>
        </Menu>

        {/* üõí –ê–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω–∞ */}
        <AnimatedCartIcon
          itemCount={cartItems.length}
          onClick={handleCartClick}
          ref={cartRef}
        />

        {/* üõ†Ô∏è –ê–¥–º–∏–Ω–∫–∞ */}
        <IconButton 
          color="inherit" 
          onClick={() => window.open('/admin', '_blank')}
          title="–ü–∞–Ω–µ–ª—å –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞"
        >
          <AdminPanelSettings />
        </IconButton>

        {/* üë§ –ü—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª—å */}
        <IconButton color="inherit" onClick={handleProfileMenu}>
          <AccountCircle />
        </IconButton>
        <Menu
          anchorEl={profileAnchor}
          open={Boolean(profileAnchor)}
          onClose={handleProfileClose}
        >
          {user && (
            <>
              <MenuItem disabled>
                {user.name ? user.name : user.email}
              </MenuItem>
              <MenuItem onClick={() => { handleProfileClose(); navigate('/orders'); }}>–ò—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑–æ–≤</MenuItem>
              <MenuItem onClick={handleLogout}>{t('logout')}</MenuItem>
            </>
          )}
        </Menu>
      </Toolbar>
    </AppBar>
  );
};

export default Header;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—é –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞—à–µ–π –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏:


```markdown
# üé® –†—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ø–æ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è–º

## üöÄ –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É

### –û–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–µ
–ü—Ä–∏ –Ω–∞–∂–∞—Ç–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ "–î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É" –∏–∑–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ –ø–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ "–ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª–µ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç" –∫ –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–µ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã, —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–Ω—ã–π –≤–∏–∑—É–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è.

### –¢–µ—Ö–Ω–æ–ª–æ–≥–∏–∏
- **React Spring** - —Å–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∞ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–π
- **TypeScript** - –ø–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è
- **Material-UI** - –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è —Å —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—â–∏–º –¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω–æ–º

### –ö–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã

#### 1. FlyingProduct.tsx
```typescript
// –ê–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞
const FlyingProduct: React.FC<FlyingProductProps> = ({
  isVisible,
  productImage,
  startPosition,
  endPosition,
  onComplete,
}) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: { x: startPosition.x, y: startPosition.y, scale: 1, opacity: 1, rotate: 0 },
    to: { x: endPosition.x, y: endPosition.y, scale: 0.3, opacity: 0, rotate: 360 },
    config: { tension: 300, friction: 20, mass: 1 },
    onRest: onComplete,
  });
  
  return <animated.img style={spring} />;
};
```

#### 2. useFlyingAnimation.ts
```typescript
// –•—É–∫ –¥–ª—è —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–µ–π
const useFlyingAnimation = () => {
  const [isFlying, setIsFlying] = useState(false);
  const [flyingPosition, setFlyingPosition] = useState({ start: null, end: null });
  
  const triggerAnimation = useCallback((image, startElement, endElement) => {
    // –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–∏ —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –∏ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é
  }, []);
  
  return { isFlying, flyingPosition, triggerAnimation, resetAnimation };
};
```

#### 3. AnimatedCartIcon.tsx
```typescript
// –ê–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∞ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã
const AnimatedCartIcon: React.FC<AnimatedCartIconProps> = ({ itemCount, onClick }) => {
  const spring = useSpring({
    scale: itemCount > 0 ? 1.1 : 1,
    rotate: itemCount > 0 ? 360 : 0,
    config: { tension: 400, friction: 10, mass: 0.8 }
  });
  
  return <animated.div style={spring}>{/* –ò–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∞ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã */}</animated.div>;
};
```

### –ò–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è

#### –í ProductCatalog.tsx
```typescript
const ProductCatalog: React.FC<ProductCatalogProps> = ({ cartRef }) => {
  const { isFlying, flyingPosition, triggerAnimation } = useFlyingAnimation();
  
  const handleAddToCart = (product, cardElement) => {
    if (cartRef.current) {
      triggerAnimation(product.image, cardElement, cartRef.current);
    }
    dispatch(addToCart(product));
  };
  
  return (
    <>
      {/* –ö–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ */}
      {isFlying && <FlyingProduct {...animationProps} />}
    </>
  );
};
```

          onClick={handleCartClick}
          ref={cartRef}
        />
      </Toolbar>
    </AppBar>
  );
};
```

    to: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },

### 2. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –º–æ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω
```typescript
// –ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –º–æ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω

### 3. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–æ–∫
```typescript
// –ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏
const AnimatedButton = ({ children, onClick }) => {
  const [spring, api] = useSpring(() => ({
    scale: 1,
    config: { tension: 400, friction: 10 }
  }));

  return (
    <animated.button
      style={spring}
      onMouseEnter={() => api.start({ scale: 1.05 })}
      onMouseLeave={() => api.start({ scale: 1 })}
      onClick={onClick}
    >
      {children}
    </animated.button>
  );
};
```

### 4. –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥–æ–≤ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–∞–º–∏

const PageTransition = ({ children, isVisible }) => {
  const spring = useSpring({

  const particles = useTrail(5, {
    from: { scale: 0, opacity: 1 },
    to: { scale: 1, opacity: 0 },
    config: { tension: 300, friction: 20 }
  });
  
  return particles.map((spring, index) => (
    <animated.div key={index} style={spring} />
  ));
};
```

- **–ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥—ã** - –í—Å–µ —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ã –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–∞ –∏–º–µ—é—Ç –ø–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏

- **3 —è–∑—ã–∫–∞** - –ò–≤—Ä–∏—Ç, –∞–Ω–≥–ª–∏–π—Å–∫–∏–π, —Ä—É—Å—Å–∫–∏–π

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–¥–∏–º –Ω–µ–±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–π —Ç–µ—Å—Ç –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏:


```typescriptreact
import React from 'react';
import { render, screen } from '@testing-library/react';
import FlyingProduct from './FlyingProduct';

// –ú–æ–∫–∞–µ–º React Spring
jest.mock('@react-spring/web', () => ({
  useSpring: () => ({
    x: 0,
    y: 0,
    scale: 1,
    opacity: 1,
    rotate: 0,
  }),
  animated: {
    img: ({ src, alt, ...props }: any) => <img src={src} alt={alt} {...props} />,
  },
}));

describe('FlyingProduct', () => {
  const mockProps = {
    isVisible: true,
    productImage: 'test-image.jpg',
    startPosition: { x: 100, y: 100 },
    endPosition: { x: 200, y: 200 },
    onComplete: jest.fn(),
  };

  it('renders when visible', () => {
    render(<FlyingProduct {...mockProps} />);
    const img = screen.getByAltText('Flying product');
    expect(img).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(img).toHaveAttribute('src', 'test-image.jpg');
  });

  it('does not render when not visible', () => {
    render(<FlyingProduct {...mockProps} isVisible={false} />);
    const img = screen.queryByAltText('Flying product');
    expect(img).not.toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('has correct styles', () => {
    render(<FlyingProduct {...mockProps} />);
    const img = screen.getByAltText('Flying product');
    expect(img).toHaveStyle({
      position: 'fixed',
      zIndex: '9999',
      width: '60px',
      height: '60px',
      objectFit: 'cover',
      borderRadius: '8px',
      pointerEvents: 'none',
    });
  });
});
```

## üéâ **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞!**

#### **3. –î–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏—è:**
- **`ANIMATION_GUIDE.md`** - –ü–æ–¥—Ä–æ–±–Ω–æ–µ —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ø–æ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è–º
- **–û–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—ë–Ω–Ω—ã–π README.md** - –ò–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—è—Ö

### üéØ **–û—Å–æ–±–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏:**

#### **–§–∏–∑–∏–∫–∞ –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω (React Spring):**
```typescript
config: {
  tension: 300,    // –ñ—ë—Å—Ç–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω—ã
  friction: 20,    // –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ
  mass: 1,         // –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞
}
```

#### **–≠—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç—ã –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏:**
- ‚úÖ **–ú–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ** - —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä —É–º–µ–Ω—å—à–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–±–ª–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –∫ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω–µ
- ‚úÖ **–ü–æ–≤–æ—Ä–æ—Ç** - —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –æ–±–æ—Ä–æ—Ç –≤–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –ø–æ–ª—ë—Ç–∞
- ‚úÖ **–ü—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** - —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–∞–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∏ –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã
- ‚úÖ **–ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω–∞—è —Ç—Ä–∞–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è** - –µ—Å—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –¥–≤–∏–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –¥—É–≥–µ

#### **–î–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–∏—è:**
- ‚úÖ **Hover —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç—ã** –Ω–∞ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–∞—Ö —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
- ‚úÖ **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∞ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã** —Å —É–≤–µ–ª–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –ø—Ä–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
- ‚úÖ **–ü–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥—ã** –¥–ª—è –≤—Å–µ—Ö –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã—Ö —ç–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤

### üöÄ **–í–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç–∏—è:**

1. **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤** - –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å –∑–∞–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–æ–π
2. **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –º–æ–¥–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–∫–æ–Ω** - –ø–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ –ø–æ—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ/–∏—Å—á–µ–∑–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏–µ
3. **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–æ–∫** - –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ hover —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç—ã
4. **–ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Ö–æ–¥–æ–≤ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–∞–º–∏** - –ø–ª–∞–≤–Ω–∞—è —Å–º–µ–Ω–∞ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∞

### üé® **–ü—Ä–µ–∏–º—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ React Spring:**

- ‚úÖ **–§–∏–∑–∏–∫–∞ –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω** - –µ—Å—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
- ‚úÖ **–ü—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** - –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥
- ‚úÖ **–ì–∏–±–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å** - –ª–µ–≥–∫–æ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä—ã
- ‚úÖ **TypeScript** - –ø–æ–ª–Ω–∞—è —Ç–∏–ø–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è
- ‚úÖ **–°–æ–æ–±—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ** - –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∫–∞

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –ø—Ä–∏ –Ω–∞–∂–∞—Ç–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ "–î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É" —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä –∫—Ä–∞—Å–∏–≤–æ "–ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª–µ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç" –∫ –∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–µ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—ã, —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏—è—Ç–Ω—ã–π –≤–∏–∑—É–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç! üéØ‚ú®

```typescript
config: {
  tension: 300,    // –ñ—ë—Å—Ç–∫–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä—É–∂–∏–Ω—ã
  friction: 20,    // –¢—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–µ
  mass: 1,         // –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞
}
```

---

**User**

–¢–∞–∫, –¥—Ä—É–∂–∏—â–µ, —Ç–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü–∞ –æ–æ–æ–æ—á–µ–Ω—å –¥–æ–ª–≥–æ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è
–ò –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–æ—á–∫–µ —è –Ω–µ –≤–∏–∂—É
–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å –∫–æ–¥ –∏ —Ä–∞–∑–±–µ—Ä–∏—Å—å, –≤ —á–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞

---

**Cursor**

–î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ä–∞–∑–±–µ—Ä—ë–º—Å—è —Å –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞–º–∏! –°–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã.


–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º –∫–æ–¥ –∏ –Ω–∞–π–¥—ë–º –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã:


–Ø –≤–∏–∂—É –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º. –î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º —Ö—É–∫ useFlyingAnimation:


–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º FlyingProduct:


–Ø –Ω–∞—à—ë–ª –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã! –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã:

1. **React Spring —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë—Ç –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –ø—Ä–∏ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–º —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–µ** - —ç—Ç–æ –∑–∞–º–µ–¥–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—É
2. **useSpring –≤—ã–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –¥–∞–∂–µ –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º**
3. **–ù–µ—Ç –º–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–ª—è —Ç—è–∂—ë–ª—ã—Ö –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π**

–î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–º —ç—Ç–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';

interface FlyingProductProps {
  isVisible: boolean;
  productImage: string;
  startPosition: { x: number; y: number };
  endPosition: { x: number; y: number };
  onComplete: () => void;
}

const FlyingProduct: React.FC<FlyingProductProps> = ({
  isVisible,
  productImage,
  startPosition,
  endPosition,
  onComplete,
}) => {
  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
  const animationConfig = useMemo(() => ({
    tension: 300,
    friction: 20,
    mass: 1,
  }), []);

  // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –≤–∏–¥–∏–º
  const spring = useSpring({
    from: {
      x: startPosition.x,
      y: startPosition.y,
      scale: 1,
      opacity: 1,
      rotate: 0,
    },
    to: {
      x: endPosition.x,
      y: endPosition.y,
      scale: 0.3,
      opacity: 0,
      rotate: 360,
    },
    config: animationConfig,
    onRest: onComplete,
    immediate: !isVisible, // –ü—Ä–æ–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º
  });

  // –ù–µ —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–∏–º –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º
  if (!isVisible) return null;

  return (
    <animated.img
      src={productImage}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        zIndex: 9999,
        width: 60,
        height: 60,
        objectFit: 'cover',
        borderRadius: 8,
        pointerEvents: 'none',
        boxShadow: '0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
        ...spring, // –í—Å–µ –∞–Ω–∏–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞
      }}
      alt="Flying product"
    />
  );
};

export default FlyingProduct;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º ProductCatalog, –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–≤ –º–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –¥–ª—è —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
import Grid from '@mui/material/Grid';
import {
  Card,
  CardMedia,
  CardContent,
  Typography,
  Button,
  Chip,
  Box,
  TextField,
  InputAdornment,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
} from '@mui/material';

import { Search, Add, Spa, Store } from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { fetchProducts, setSearchTerm, setSelectedCategory } from '../../store/slices/productsSlice';
import { addToCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { Product, ProductCategory } from '../../types';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useFlyingAnimation } from '../../hooks/useFlyingAnimation';
import FlyingProduct from '../common/FlyingProduct';

interface ProductCatalogProps {
  cartRef: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>;
}

const ProductCatalog: React.FC<ProductCatalogProps> = ({ cartRef }) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const { items, loading, selectedCategory, searchTerm } = useAppSelector(state => state.products);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  
  // –•—É–∫ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞
  const {
    isFlying,
    flyingPosition,
    productImage,
    triggerAnimation,
    resetAnimation,
  } = useFlyingAnimation();

  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchProducts());
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
  const filteredProducts = useMemo(() => {
    return items.filter(product => {
      const p = product as any;
      const matchesCategory = !selectedCategory || p.category === selectedCategory;
      const search = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
      const matchesSearch =
        (typeof p.nameRu === 'string' && p.nameRu.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
        (typeof p.nameEn === 'string' && p.nameEn.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
        (typeof p.nameHe === 'string' && p.nameHe.includes(search));
      return matchesCategory && matchesSearch;
    });
  }, [items, selectedCategory, searchTerm]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
  const handleAddToCart = useCallback((product: Product, cardElement: HTMLElement) => {
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é
    if (cartRef.current) {
      triggerAnimation(product.image, cardElement, cartRef.current);
    }
    
    // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
    dispatch(addToCart(product));
  }, [cartRef, triggerAnimation, dispatch]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—é –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è —ç–º–æ–¥–∑–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–µ–≥–æ—Ä–∏–∏
  const getCategoryEmoji = useCallback((category: ProductCategory) => {
    const emojis = {
      [ProductCategory.VEGETABLES]: 'ü•¨',
      [ProductCategory.FRUITS]: 'üçé',
      [ProductCategory.HERBS]: 'üåø',
      [ProductCategory.DAIRY]: 'ü•õ',
      [ProductCategory.HONEY]: 'üçØ',
      [ProductCategory.FLOWERS]: 'üå∏',
    };
    return emojis[category] || 'üåæ';
  }, []);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∏–π —è–∑—ã–∫
  const lang = useMemo(() => i18n.language || 'en', [i18n.language]);

  return (
    <Box sx={{ padding: 3 }}>
      {/* üîç –§–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä—ã */}
      <Box sx={{ mb: 3, display: 'flex', gap: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
        <TextField
          placeholder={t('search_products')}
          value={searchTerm}
          onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSearchTerm(e.target.value))}
          InputProps={{
            startAdornment: (
              <InputAdornment position="start">
                <Search />
              </InputAdornment>
            ),
          }}
          sx={{
            minWidth: 300,
            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.85)',
            boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)',
            borderRadius: 2,
            '& .MuiInputBase-root': {
              borderRadius: 2,
              background: 'transparent',
            },
          }}
        />
        
        <FormControl sx={{ minWidth: 200 }}>
          <InputLabel>{t('category')}</InputLabel>
          <Select
            value={selectedCategory || ''}
            onChange={(e) => dispatch(setSelectedCategory(e.target.value as ProductCategory || null))}
            label={t('category')}
          >
            <MenuItem value="">{t('all_categories')}</MenuItem>
            {Object.values(ProductCategory).map((category) => (
              <MenuItem key={category} value={category}>
                {getCategoryEmoji(category)} {category}
              </MenuItem>
            ))}
          </Select>
        </FormControl>
      </Box>

      {/* üì¶ –ö–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ–≥ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤ */}
      <Grid container spacing={3} justifyContent="center">
        {filteredProducts.map((product) => {
          const p = product as any; // –¥–ª—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –∫ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º –ø–æ–ª—è–º
          const name =
            (typeof p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`name${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.nameEn || p.nameRu || p.nameHe || '';
          const description =
            (typeof p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`] === 'string' && p[`description${lang.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + lang.slice(1)}`]) ||
            p.descriptionEn || p.descriptionRu || p.descriptionHe || '';
          
          return (
            <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} md={4} lg={3} key={p.id}>
              <Card 
                sx={{ 
                  height: '100%', 
                  display: 'flex', 
                  flexDirection: 'column',
                  transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.2s ease-in-out',
                  '&:hover': {
                    transform: 'translateY(-4px)',
                    boxShadow: '0 8px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
                  }
                }}
              >
                <CardMedia
                  component="img"
                  height="200"
                  image={p.image}
                  alt={name}
                />
                <CardContent sx={{ flexGrow: 1 }}>
                  <Typography variant="h6" component="h2" gutterBottom>
                    {getCategoryEmoji(p.category)} {name}
                  </Typography>
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" gutterBottom>
                    {description}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1, mb: 2, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                    {p.organic && (
                      <Chip icon={<Spa />} label="Organic" size="small" color="success" />
                    )}
                    <Chip icon={<Store />} label={p.farmName} size="small" variant="outlined" />
                  </Box>
                  
                  <Typography variant="h6" color="primary" gutterBottom>
                    ‚Ç™{p.price} / {p.unit}
                  </Typography>
                  
                  <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary">
                    üìç {p.location}
                  </Typography>
                </CardContent>
                
                <Box sx={{ p: 2, pt: 0 }}>
                  <Button
                    fullWidth
                    variant="contained"
                    startIcon={<Add />}
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      const cardElement = e.currentTarget.closest('.MuiCard-root') as HTMLElement;
                      if (cardElement) {
                        handleAddToCart(product, cardElement);
                      }
                    }}
                    disabled={!product.inStock}
                    sx={{ 
                      backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
                      transition: 'all 0.2s ease-in-out',
                      '&:hover': {
                        backgroundColor: '#45a049',
                        transform: 'scale(1.02)',
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    {product.inStock ? t('add_to_cart') : '◊ê◊ñ◊ú ◊ë◊û◊ú◊ê◊ô Out of Stock'}
                  </Button>
                </Box>
              </Card>
            </Grid>
          );
        })}
      </Grid>

      {/* üéØ –ê–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞ —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–∞ */}
      {isFlying && flyingPosition.start && flyingPosition.end && productImage && (
        <FlyingProduct
          isVisible={isFlying}
          productImage={productImage}
          startPosition={flyingPosition.start}
          endPosition={flyingPosition.end}
          onComplete={resetAnimation}
        />
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default ProductCatalog;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º AnimatedCartIcon:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useMemo } from 'react';
import { useSpring, animated } from '@react-spring/web';
import { Badge, IconButton } from '@mui/material';
import { ShoppingCart } from '@mui/icons-material';

interface AnimatedCartIconProps {
  itemCount: number;
  onClick: () => void;
  ref?: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement>;
}

const AnimatedCartIcon: React.FC<AnimatedCartIconProps> = ({ 
  itemCount, 
  onClick, 
  ref 
}) => {
  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
  const animationConfig = useMemo(() => ({
    tension: 400,
    friction: 10,
    mass: 0.8
  }), []);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏
  const animationValues = useMemo(() => ({
    scale: itemCount > 0 ? 1.1 : 1,
    rotate: itemCount > 0 ? 360 : 0,
  }), [itemCount]);

  const spring = useSpring({
    ...animationValues,
    config: animationConfig
  });

  return (
    <animated.div style={spring}>
      <IconButton 
        ref={ref}
        color="inherit" 
        onClick={onClick}
        sx={{
          transition: 'all 0.2s ease-in-out',
          '&:hover': {
            transform: 'scale(1.05)',
          }
        }}
      >
        <Badge badgeContent={itemCount} color="error">
          <ShoppingCart />
        </Badge>
      </IconButton>
    </animated.div>
  );
};

export default AnimatedCartIcon;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º, –µ—Å—Ç—å –ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã —Å –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–æ–π –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏–º productsSlice:


–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –≤ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑ Firebase –ø—Ä–∏ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–º —Ä–µ–Ω–¥–µ—Ä–µ. –î–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫—É:


```typescript
import { createSlice, createAsyncThunk, PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { Product, ProductCategory } from '../../types';
import { db } from '../../firebase';
import { collection, getDocs } from 'firebase/firestore';

interface ProductsState {
  items: Product[];
  loading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  selectedCategory: ProductCategory | null;
  searchTerm: string;
  lastFetched: number | null; // –í—Ä–µ–º—è –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ–π –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏
}

const initialState: ProductsState = {
  items: [],
  loading: false,
  error: null,
  selectedCategory: null,
  searchTerm: '',
  lastFetched: null,
};

// üåê –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —ç–∫—à–µ–Ω –¥–ª—è –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç–æ–≤ —Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º
export const fetchProducts = createAsyncThunk(
  'products/fetchProducts',
  async (_, { getState }) => {
    const state = getState() as { products: ProductsState };
    const { lastFetched } = state.products;
    
    // –ö—ç—à–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–∞ 5 –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç
    const CACHE_DURATION = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç
    const now = Date.now();
    
    // –ï—Å–ª–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω—ã –Ω–µ–¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ, –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ–º –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
    if (lastFetched && (now - lastFetched) < CACHE_DURATION) {
      return state.products.items;
    }
    
    try {
      // –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–∑ Firestore
      const querySnapshot = await getDocs(collection(db, 'products'));
      const products: Product[] = [];
      
      querySnapshot.forEach((doc) => {
        const data = doc.data();
        products.push({
          id: doc.id,
          name: data.name,
          nameEn: data.nameEn,
          nameRu: data.nameRu,
          nameHe: data.nameHe,
          price: data.price,
          currency: 'ILS',
          category: data.category,
          description: data.description,
          descriptionEn: data.descriptionEn,
          descriptionRu: data.descriptionRu,
          descriptionHe: data.descriptionHe,
          image: data.image,
          farmId: data.farmId || '',
          farmName: data.farmName,
          location: data.location,
          organic: data.organic,
          inStock: data.inStock,
          unit: data.unit
        });
      });
      
      return products;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–¥—É–∫—Ç–æ–≤:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
);

const productsSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'products',
  initialState,
  reducers: {
    setSelectedCategory: (state, action: PayloadAction<ProductCategory | null>) => {
      state.selectedCategory = action.payload;
    },
    setSearchTerm: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {
      state.searchTerm = action.payload;
    },
    clearFilters: (state) => {
      state.selectedCategory = null;
      state.searchTerm = '';
    },
  },
  extraReducers: (builder) => {
    builder
      .addCase(fetchProducts.pending, (state) => {
        state.loading = true;
        state.error = null;
      })
      .addCase(fetchProducts.fulfilled, (state, action) => {
        state.loading = false;
        state.items = action.payload;
        state.lastFetched = Date.now();
      })
      .addCase(fetchProducts.rejected, (state, action) => {
        state.loading = false;
        state.error = action.error.message || 'Failed to fetch products';
      });
  },
});

export const { setSelectedCategory, setSearchTerm, clearFilters } = productsSlice.actions;
export default productsSlice.reducer;
```

–¢–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –¥–∞–≤–∞–π—Ç–µ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º –∏–Ω–¥–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –≤ ProductCatalog:


```typescriptreact
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useCallback } from 'react';
import Grid from '@mui/material/Grid';
import {
  Card,
  CardMedia,
  CardContent,
  Typography,
  Button,
  Chip,
  Box,
  TextField,
  InputAdornment,
  FormControl,
  InputLabel,
  Select,
  MenuItem,
  CircularProgress,
  Alert,
} from '@mui/material';

import { Search, Add, Spa, Store } from '@mui/icons-material';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '../../hooks/redux';
import { fetchProducts, setSearchTerm, setSelectedCategory } from '../../store/slices/productsSlice';
import { addToCart } from '../../store/slices/cartSlice';
import { Product, ProductCategory } from '../../types';
import { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';
import i18n from '../../i18n';
import { useFlyingAnimation } from '../../hooks/useFlyingAnimation';
import FlyingProduct from '../common/FlyingProduct';

interface ProductCatalogProps {
  cartRef: React.RefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>;
}

const ProductCatalog: React.FC<ProductCatalogProps> = ({ cartRef }) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const { items, loading, error, selectedCategory, searchTerm } = useAppSelector(state => state.products);
  const { t } = useTranslation();
  
  // –•—É–∫ –¥–ª—è –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ª—ë—Ç–∞
  const {
    isFlying,
    flyingPosition,
    productImage,
    triggerAnimation,
    resetAnimation,
  } = useFlyingAnimation();

  useEffect(() => {
    dispatch(fetchProducts());
  }, [dispatch]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ñ–∏–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—é —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä–æ–≤
  const filteredProducts = useMemo(() => {
    return items.filter(product => {
      const p = product as any;
      const matchesCategory = !selectedCategory || p.category === selectedCategory;
      const search = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
      const matchesSearch =
        (typeof p.nameRu === 'string' && p.nameRu.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
        (typeof p.nameEn === 'string' && p.nameEn.toLowerCase().includes(search)) ||
        (typeof p.nameHe === 'string' && p.nameHe.includes(search));
      return matchesCategory && matchesSearch;
    });
  }, [items, selectedCategory, searchTerm]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
  const handleAddToCart = useCallback((product: Product, cardElement: HTMLElement) => {
    // –ó–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞–µ–º –∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ü–∏—é
    if (cartRef.current) {
      triggerAnimation(product.image, cardElement, cartRef.current);
    }
    
    // –î–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º –≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∑–∏–Ω—É
    dispatch(addToCart(product));
  }, [cartRef, triggerAnimation, dispatch]);

  // –ú–µ–º–æ–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—é –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏—è —ç–º–æ–¥–∑–∏ –∫–∞—Ç–µ–≥–æ—Ä–∏–∏
  const getCategoryEmoji = useCallback((category: ProductCategory) => {
    const emojis = {
      [ProductCategory.VEGETABLES]: 'ü•¨',
      [ProductCategory.FRUITS]: 'üçé',
      [ProductCategory.HERBS]: 'üåø',
      [ProductCategory.DAIRY]: 'ü•õ',
      [ProductCategory.HONEY]: 'üçØ',
      [ProductCategory.FLOWERS]: 'üå∏',
    };
    return emojis[category] || 'üåæ';
  }, []);
